$1.80</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;padding-left:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">NORTH CANTON, Ohio - Diebold, Incorporated (NYSE: DBD) today reported </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2014 net income attributable to Diebold of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$33.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$0.51</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;per share. </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">This compares with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2013 net loss of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$(21.7) million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$(0.34)</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;per share, including a pre-tax goodwill impairment charge in Brazil of $70 million, or ($0.84) per share. </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">Third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2014 revenue was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$768.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, up 8.9% from the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2013, or 9.3% on a constant currency basis.   </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Non-GAAP* income attributable to Diebold in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2014 was $0.54 per share, compared with $0.56 per share in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2013.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Management Commentary</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:0px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#8220;We delivered another solid quarter as we continue to execute on our turnaround strategy, evidenced by strong revenue growth and gross margin expansion from the third quarter last year,&#8221; said Andy W. Mattes, Diebold president and chief executive officer. &#8220;As planned, our operational results enabled us to ramp up reinvestments back into the business during the quarter.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:0px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:0px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#8220;We will further increase our investments in the fourth quarter, focusing on areas such as research and development,&#8221; Mattes continued.  &#8220;These reinvestments are starting to pay dividends.  For example, we recently launched the Diebold 5500, a new line of cash dispensers and our first all-new product line in a number of years.  Unveiled in London earlier this month, the 5500 is geared toward the mass market in key international regions and provides a lower total cost of ownership for the ATM deployer. We will be following this up with several new solution launches in the coming months. Consistently and quickly bringing new innovation to the market is an important part of our turnaround strategy.&#8221;  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:0px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:0px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Mattes concluded, &#8220;We continue to execute relative to our transformation efforts and are showing proof points. As such, we are narrowing our earnings guidance around the center of our previously reported range.  We feel good about the progress we've made to date as we begin to eye the &#8216;walk&#8217; phase of our &#8216;crawl, walk, run&#8217; turnaround."   </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;">Gross Margin </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Total gross margin for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2014 was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">26.1%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, an increase of 1.6 percentage points from the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter of 2013, with service margin reflecting a 1.9 percentage point improvement and product margin increasing 2.0 percentage points.  The service margin improvement was primarily attributable to the company's global service transformation efforts.  The product gross margin increase was primarily the result of geographic mix.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;">Operating Expenses</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Total operating expenses were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$153.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, or </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">20.0%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;of revenue, for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2014, compared with $203.1 million, or 28.8% of revenue, in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter of 2013. Operating expenses in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2013 included $75.7 million of restructuring and non-routine charges, comprised primarily of $70.0 million related to the Brazil goodwill impairment.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font compared with</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$48.0 million, or 6.8% of revenue, in the </font><font style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;">Income Tax</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">The effective tax rate on continuing operations for the three months ended September 30, 2014 was 27.0%, compared with 28.2% for the same period of 2013. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;">Net Income / (Loss) Attributable to Diebold</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Net income attributable to Diebold was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$33.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, or 4.3% of revenue, in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2014, compared with net loss of ($21.7) million, or (3.1%) of revenue, in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2013.  Included in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2013 net of tax results were $54.3 million of net non-routine and amortization expenses, $53.7 million of which related to the establishment of a valuation allowance on certain Brazil deferred tax assets, and $3.4 million in restructuring costs.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Balance Sheet, Cash Flow and Liquidity</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">The company's net debt* was $264.5 million at </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">September&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, an increase in net debt of $213.7 million from the net debt* position at </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">December&#160;31, 2013</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">.  The company's net debt to capital ratio was 21.0% at </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">September&#160;30, 2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, 4.5% at </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">December&#160;31, 2013</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;and 14.7% at September 30, 2013.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Free cash flow (use)* in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2014 was ($34.2) million, compared with ($3.1) million in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;quarter 2013.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Full-year 2014 Outlook</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">The following statements are based on current expectations.  These statements are forward-looking and actual results may differ materially. These statements do not include the potential impact of significant currency fluctuations, future mergers, acquisitions, disposals or other business combinations, the Brazil tax assessment or related indirect tax reserves.    </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">The company is updating its outlook for full-year 2014 revenue to grow approximately 7% and EPS to be in the range of $1.70 to $1.80 on a non-GAAP* basis.  The current guidance now assumes a full-year, non-GAAP effective tax rate of approximately 32%, compared with previous guidance which assumed an approximate 30% full-year, non-GAAP effective tax rate. Diebold is focused on executing its transformation initiatives and increasing investment levels in the areas of development, sales and marketing, information technology and back-end office support. style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Notes for Non-GAAP Measures</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">To supplement our condensed consolidated financial statements presented in accordance with GAAP, the company considers certain financial measures that are not prepared in accordance with GAAP, including non-GAAP results, adjusted earnings per share, free cash flow/(use) and net investment/(debt).  The company uses these non-GAAP financial measures, in addition to GAAP financial measures, to evaluate our operating and financial performance and to compare such performance to that of prior periods and to the performance of our competitors.  Also, the company uses these non-GAAP financial measures in making operational and financial decisions and in establishing operational goals.  The company also believes providing these non-GAAP financial measures to investors, as a supplement to GAAP financial measures, helps investors evaluate our operating and financial performance and trends in our business, consistent with how management evaluates such performance and trends.  The company also believes these non-GAAP financial measures may be useful to investors in comparing its performance to the performance of other companies, although its non-GAAP financial measures are specific to the company and the non-GAAP financial measures of other companies may not be calculated in the same manner.  </font></div><div organization for research and development, as well as transforming the company's general and administrative cost structure. Non-routine expenses relate to the settlement of the FCPA investigation and securities class action lawsuit, Brazil impairment, and the legal, indemnification and professional fees paid by the company in connection with ongoing obligations related to prior regulatory settlements.  Non-routine tax expense (benefit) on foreign cash repatriation relates to the 2013 change in assertion regarding the indefinite reinvestment of foreign subsidiary earnings.</font></div><div
